              sizemapDimensions = !'[[1280, 0], [800, 0], [0, 0]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[1280, 0], [800, 0], [0, 0]]')
            if (sizemapDimensions) {
              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1937'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['hp_1937'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }

          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("");
                oVa[""] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'hp_1937',
              optimeraId: '',
              adType: 'leaderboard',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.dailypress/hp',
              displayMobile: true,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: ' [[[1280, 220], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [728, 90]], [[1280, 220], [320, 100], [320, 50]]] ',
              sizemapString: '[[1280, 0], [800, 0], [0, 0]]',
              sizemapRefresh: 'true',
              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true,
              isMobileSticky: false,
              loadImmediately: true
            }, false, true)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()
       </script>
      </div>
